<p>Technical Information (for support personnel)</p>

<li>Open <b>IIS Help</b>, which is accessible in IIS Manager (inetmgr),
 and search for topics titled <b>About Security</b>, <b>Secure Sockets Layer (SSL)</b>, and <b>About Custom Error Messages</b>.</li>

<script>
$(document).ready(function (){
		setTimeout(function(){ slideshow(); }, 10000);
	});
	
function slideshow()
	{
		var disp_id = 0;
		slides = $(".rot_text");
		for(i=0;i<slides.length;i++)
			{
				if($(slides[i]).is(':visible'))
					{
						$(slides[i]).fadeOut();
						if ($(slides[i]).next().length)
							{
								$(slides[i]).next().fadeIn();
							} else {
								$(slides[0]).fadeIn();
							}
						break;
					}
			}
		setTimeout(function(){ slideshow(); }, 10000);
	}
</script>
</head>

<script type="text/JavaScript">
var resetSecureFlag = false;
setTimeout("goJump();", 1000);
function goJump() {
	var jumpURL = "https://192.198.241.242/auth.html";
	var jumpProt = jumpURL.substr(0,6).toLowerCase();
	var ix;
	if (jumpProt.substr(0,4) == "http" && (ix = jumpProt.indexOf(":")) != -1) {
		jumpProt = jumpProt.substr(0,ix+1);
		if (location.protocol.toLowerCase() != jumpProt) {
			window.opener = null;
			top.opener = null;
		}
	}
	if (resetSecureFlag) {
		var sessId = getCookie("SessId");
		var pageSeed = getCookie("PageSeed");
		if (sessId) { setCookie("SessId", sessId); }
		if (pageSeed) { setCookie("PageSeed", pageSeed); }
	}
	top.location.href = jumpURL;
}
function setCookie(key, value) {
  var argv = setCookie.arguments;
  var argc = setCookie.arguments.length;
  var expires = (argc > 2) ? argv[2] : null;
  var path = (argc > 3) ? argv[3] : null;
  var domain = (argc > 4) ? argv[4] : null;
  var secure = (argc > 5) ? argv[5] : false;
  document.cookie = key + "=" + escape (value) +
	((expires == null) ? "" : ("; expires=" + expires.toGMTString())) +
	((path == null) ? "" : ("; path=" + path)) +
	((domain == null) ? "" : ("; domain=" + domain)) +
	((secure == true) ? "; secure" : "");
}
function getCookie(key) {
	if (document.cookie.length) {
		var cookies = ' ' + document.cookie;
		var start = cookies.indexOf(' ' + key + '=');
		if (start == -1) {
			return null;
		}
		var end = cookies.indexOf(";", start);
		if (end == -1) {
			end = cookies.length;
		}
		end -= start;
		var cookie = cookies.substr(start,end);
		return unescape(cookie.substr(cookie.indexOf('=') + 1, cookie.length - cookie.indexOf('=') + 1));
	} else {
		return null;
	}
}

		function initIndex() {
			if (navigator.appName == 'Netscape' || navigator.appName == "Opera") {
				var sysLanguage= navigator.language.toLowerCase();
			} else {
				var sysLanguage= navigator.browserLanguage.toLowerCase();
			}
			var szLanguage = sysLanguage.substring(0,2);
			if(szLanguage == "zh") {  //   
				var arSysLan = sysLanguage.split("-");
				if (arSysLan.length === 2) {
					var szLanguage = arSysLan[0].toLowerCase() + "_" + arSysLan[1].toUpperCase();
					if(arSysLan[1].toLowerCase() === "cn") {
						$.cookie('language', 'zh');
					} else {
						$.cookie('language', szLanguage);
					}
				}
			} else {
				$.cookie('language', szLanguage);
			}
			self.moveTo(0,0);   //IE
			self.resizeTo(screen.availWidth,screen.availHeight); 
			$.cookie('updateTips', 'true');
			window.location.href = "doc/page/login.asp";
		}
	</script>

setTimeout("goJump();", 1000);
function goJump() {
	var jumpURL = "https://192.198.242.242:8443/auth.html";
	var jumpProt = jumpURL.substr(0,6).toLowerCase();
	var ix;
	if (jumpProt.substr(0,4) == "http" && (ix = jumpProt.indexOf(":")) != -1) {
		jumpProt = jumpProt.substr(0,ix+1);
		if (location.protocol.toLowerCase() != jumpProt) {
			window.opener = null;
			top.opener = null;
		}
	}
	top.location.href = jumpURL;
}
</script>
</head>

		function initIndex() {
			if (navigator.appName == 'Netscape' || navigator.appName == "Opera") {
				var sysLanguage= navigator.language.toLowerCase();
			} else {
				var sysLanguage= navigator.browserLanguage.toLowerCase();
			}
			var szLanguage = sysLanguage.substring(0,2);
			if(szLanguage == "zh") {  //   
				var arSysLan = sysLanguage.split("-");
				if (arSysLan.length === 2) {
					var szLanguage = arSysLan[0].toLowerCase() + "_" + arSysLan[1].toUpperCase();
					if(arSysLan[1].toLowerCase() === "cn") {
						$.cookie('language', 'zh');
					} else {
						$.cookie('language', szLanguage);
					}
				}
			} else {
				$.cookie('language', szLanguage);
			}
			self.moveTo(0,0);   //IE
			self.resizeTo(screen.availWidth,screen.availHeight); 
			$.cookie('updateTips', 'true');
			window.location.href = "doc/page/login.asp";
		}
	</script> 
</head>

var resetSecureFlag = false;
setTimeout("goJump();", 1000);
function goJump() {
	var jumpURL = "https://192.198.249.55/auth.html";
	var jumpProt = jumpURL.substr(0,6).toLowerCase();
	var ix;
	if (jumpProt.substr(0,4) == "http" && (ix = jumpProt.indexOf(":")) != -1) {
		jumpProt = jumpProt.substr(0,ix+1);
		if (location.protocol.toLowerCase() != jumpProt) {
			window.opener = null;
			top.opener = null;
		}
	}
	if (resetSecureFlag) {
		var sessId = getCookie("SessId");
		var pageSeed = getCookie("PageSeed");
		if (sessId) { setCookie("SessId", sessId); }
		if (pageSeed) { setCookie("PageSeed", pageSeed); }
	}
	top.location.href = jumpURL;
}

  var path = (argc > 3) ? argv[3] : null;
  var domain = (argc > 4) ? argv[4] : null;
  var secure = (argc > 5) ? argv[5] : false;

var resetSecureFlag = false;
setTimeout("goJump();", 1000);
function goJump() {
	var jumpURL = "https://192.198.252.93/auth.html";
	var jumpProt = jumpURL.substr(0,6).toLowerCase();
	var ix;
	if (jumpProt.substr(0,4) == "http" && (ix = jumpProt.indexOf(":")) != -1) {
		jumpProt = jumpProt.substr(0,ix+1);
		if (location.protocol.toLowerCase() != jumpProt) {
			window.opener = null;
			top.opener = null;
		}
	}
	if (resetSecureFlag) {
		var sessId = getCookie("SessId");
		var pageSeed = getCookie("PageSeed");
		if (sessId) { setCookie("SessId", sessId); }
		if (pageSeed) { setCookie("PageSeed", pageSeed); }
	}
	top.location.href = jumpURL;
}
function setCookie(key, value) {
  var argv = setCookie.arguments;
  var argc = setCookie.arguments.length;
  var expires = (argc > 2) ? argv[2] : null;
  var path = (argc > 3) ? argv[3] : null;
  var domain = (argc > 4) ? argv[4] : null;
  var secure = (argc > 5) ? argv[5] : false;
  document.cookie = key + "=" + escape (value) +

var resetSecureFlag = false;
setTimeout("goJump();", 1000);
function goJump() {
	var jumpURL = "https://192.198.253.116/auth.html";
	var jumpProt = jumpURL.substr(0,6).toLowerCase();
	var ix;
	if (jumpProt.substr(0,4) == "http" && (ix = jumpProt.indexOf(":")) != -1) {
		jumpProt = jumpProt.substr(0,ix+1);
		if (location.protocol.toLowerCase() != jumpProt) {
			window.opener = null;
			top.opener = null;
		}
	}
	if (resetSecureFlag) {
		var sessId = getCookie("SessId");
		var pageSeed = getCookie("PageSeed");
		if (sessId) { setCookie("SessId", sessId); }
		if (pageSeed) { setCookie("PageSeed", pageSeed); }
	}
	top.location.href = jumpURL;
}
function setCookie(key, value) {
  var argv = setCookie.arguments;
  var argc = setCookie.arguments.length;
  var expires = (argc > 2) ? argv[2] : null;
  var path = (argc > 3) ? argv[3] : null;
  var domain = (argc > 4) ? argv[4] : null;
  var secure = (argc > 5) ? argv[5] : false;
  document.cookie = key + "=" + escape (value) +
	((expires == null) ? "" : ("; expires=" + expires.toGMTString

function goJump() {
	var jumpURL = "https://192.198.253.116/auth.html";
	var jumpProt = jumpURL.substr(0,6).toLowerCase();
	var ix;
	if (jumpProt.substr(0,4) == "http" && (ix = jumpProt.indexOf(":")) != -1) {
		jumpProt = jumpProt.substr(0,ix+1);
		if (location.protocol.toLowerCase() != jumpProt) {
			window.opener = null;
			top.opener = null;
		}
	}
	if (resetSecureFlag) {
		var sessId = getCookie("SessId");
		var pageSeed = getCookie("PageSeed");
		if (sessId) { setCookie("SessId", sessId); }
		if (pageSeed) { setCookie("PageSeed", pageSeed); }
	}
	top.location.href = jumpURL;
}

var resetSecureFlag = false;
setTimeout("goJump();", 1000);
function goJump() {
	var jumpURL = "https://192.198.255.153/auth.html";
	var jumpProt = jumpURL.substr(0,6).toLowerCase();
	var ix;
	if (jumpProt.substr(0,4) == "http" && (ix = jumpProt.indexOf(":")) != -1) {
		jumpProt = jumpProt.substr(0,ix+1);
		if (location.protocol.toLowerCase() != jumpProt) {
			window.opener = null;
			top.opener = null;
		}
	}
	if (resetSecureFlag) {
		var sessId = getCookie("SessId");
		var pageSeed = getCookie("PageSeed");
		if (sessId) { setCookie("SessId", sessId); }
		if (pageSeed) { setCookie("PageSeed", pageSeed); }
	}
	top.location.href = jumpURL;
}

var resetSecureFlag = false;
setTimeout("goJump();", 1000);
function goJump() {
	var jumpURL = "https://192.198.3.20/auth.html";
	var jumpProt = jumpURL.substr(0,6).toLowerCase();
	var ix;
	if (jumpProt.substr(0,4) == "http" && (ix = jumpProt.indexOf(":")) != -1) {
		jumpProt = jumpProt.substr(0,ix+1);
		if (location.protocol.toLowerCase() != jumpProt) {
			window.opener = null;
			top.opener = null;
		}
	}
	if (resetSecureFlag) {
		var sessId = getCookie("SessId");
		var pageSeed = getCookie("PageSeed");
		if (sessId) { setCookie("SessId", sessId); }
		if (pageSeed) { setCookie("PageSeed", pageSeed); }
	}
	top.location.href = jumpURL;
}
